<!-- PageBreak END --><!-- Item START -->
<P ALIGN="LEFT">
<FONT SIZE="2">
<B>
	Item 2.01. Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets.
</B>
</FONT>
</P>
<P ALIGN="LEFT">
<FONT SIZE="2">
On December 21, 2004, Chordiant Software, Inc. ("Chordiant") completed its acquisition of all the issued shares of KiQ Limited, a privately held United Kingdom software company ("KiQ").  On December 8, 2004, Chordiant Software International, Inc. ("Chordiant International"), a wholly-owned subsidiary of Chordiant, entered into a share purchase agreement (the "Purchase Agreement") with Rob Walker, David Barrow, Colin Baker, Zukke Spijkers B.V. and the persons or entities represented by Commonwealth Investments B.V. (the "Shareholders"), the holders of all of the issued shares of KiQ. In addition, on December 8, 2004, Chordiant International and KiQ entered into a Trust Deed (the "Trust Deed").<br><br>The Purchase Agreement provided for Chordiant International's acquisition from the Shareholders of all the issued shares of KiQ (the "Acquisition") for an aggregate purchase price of approximately $19.1 million, consisting of (i) approximately $8.6 million in cash (of which $150,000 consisted of reimbursement to 
KiQ of certain non transaction related expenses incurred by KiQ for the benefit of Chordiant) and (ii) unregistered shares of Chordiant common stock (the "Consideration Shares") having an aggregate issue price of $9.5 million. In addition, under the Trust Deed, Chordiant agreed to pay approximately $1.05 million for certain expenses relating to the cancellation of options held by certain employees and a consultant of KiQ.  Cash in the amount of $685,000 was transferred to Chordiant by KiQ at the close of the transaction.<br><br>At the closing of the Acquisition, (i) $1,032,410 of the cash and (ii) Consideration Shares having an issue price of $1,140,000 were paid into an escrow account. The cash and Consideration Shares held in the escrow account, to the extent not used to satisfy certain limited indemnification and warranty obligations of the Shareholders, will be released to the Shareholders in three equal installments on the six month, twelve month and eighteen month anniversaries of the closing date of t
he Acquisition. <br><br>The descriptions of the Purchase Agreement and Trust Deed are not complete and are qualified in their entirety by reference to the text of such agreements, which are attached hereto as Exhibits 2.4 and 2.5, respectively.<br>
</FONT>
</P>
<!-- Item END -->
<BR><BR><BR><BR><!-- Item START -->
<P ALIGN="LEFT">
<FONT SIZE="2">
<B>
	Item 9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits.
</B>
</FONT>
</P>
<P ALIGN="LEFT">
<FONT SIZE="2">
(a)	Financial Statements of Business Acquired.<br><br>Chordiant intends to file KiQ&#x2019;s financial statements under cover of Form 8-K/A no later than 71 calendar days after the date this report is required to be filed.  <br><br>(b)	Pro Forma Financial Statements.<br><br>Chordiant intends to file pro forma financial information relating to its acquisition of KiQ under cover of Form 8-K/A no later than 71 calendar days after the date this report is required to be filed.<br><br>	(c)	Exhibits.<br><br>Exhibit No.		<br>2.4		Share Purchase Agreement, dated December 8, 2004, between Chordiant Software International, Inc. and the persons named therein[1] <br>2.5		Deed of Trust, dated December 8, 2004, between Chordiant Software International, Inc. and KiQ Limited.<br>		<br><br>[1]  Chordiant has omitted Schedules 2-4 and 7-9 to the Share Purchase Agreement pursuant to Item 601(b)(2) of Regulation S-K.  A brief description of the omitted schedules is contained in Exhibit 2.4.  Chordiant hereby undertakes to provid
e the SEC with copies of the omitted schedules upon request.<br>
</FONT>
</P>

that under Rule&nbsp;144, the Consideration Shares must be held for at least one (1)&nbsp;year after

Rule&nbsp;144 include among other things the availability of public current information about

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>3.&nbsp;CONDITIONS PRECEDENT</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">3.1. Completion of the sale and purchase of the Shares is conditional on:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">7.2. The Independent Accountants shall act on the following basis:

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>8.&nbsp;ESCROW ACCOUNT</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">8.1.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Escrow Account shall be operated, and the Escrow Sum and interest accruing on it shall be
applied, in accordance with this clause 8 and the Escrow Agreement.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">8.2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Any amount due to the Purchaser in respect of an adjustment to the Consideration, a Warranty
Claim or otherwise under this Agreement, the Share Repurchase Agreement or under the Tax Deed
shall, on becoming due, be paid to the Purchaser out of the Escrow Account to the extent of
the Escrow Sum for which purpose in first instance the cash amount will be used.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">8.3.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Subject to any amounts referred to in clause 8.2 being paid and, in the case of the
Executives, subject to the provisions of the Share Repurchase Agreement, one third of the
Escrow Sum (and for the avoidance of doubt, that shall mean one third of the Cash
Consideration and one third of the Consideration Shares) (each such third being &#147;<U>Escrow
Tranche</U>&#148;) shall be paid to the Sellers in their Relevant Proportions on each of the six
month, one year and 18&nbsp;month anniversaries of the date of Completion (each, a &#147;<U>Release
Date</U>&#148;), <U>provided that</U> no payment shall be made on a Release Date if on such date a
Warranty Claim or a claim under the Tax Deed (or in the case of the Executives, a claim under
the Share Repurchase Agreement) is outstanding.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">8.4. If such a claim is outstanding:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a sum equal to the Escrow Tranche otherwise due on such release date (or such
lesser sum as equals the current value of the Warranty Claim) shall be retained in the
Escrow Account; and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any sum so retained in the Escrow Account after the Release Date in respect of
any such claim shall be released to the Seller or the Purchaser, as appropriate, as
soon as practicable after that claim is settled.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">8.5. For the purposes of this clause, a claim shall be regarded as settled if:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">(a)&nbsp;the claim is withdrawn; or



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">(b)&nbsp;the Seller and the Purchaser so agree in writing; or


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a competent court has awarded judgment in respect of the claim and, where
relevant, the period for lodging an appeal has expired without an appeal having been
lodged.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">8.6.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Any interest which accrues on the Escrow Sum while in the Escrow Account shall follow the
principal amount and shall be paid to the Sellers in the Relevant Proportions or the Purchaser
(as the case may be) at the same time as payment of the corresponding principal.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">8.7. Each of the Sellers and the Purchaser shall:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>on Completion, give the Sellers&#146; Solicitors and the Purchaser&#146;s Solicitors
joint instructions regarding the operation of the Escrow Account in the Agreed Form;
and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">12.4.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If any of those restrictions is void but would be valid if some part of the restrictions
were deleted, the restriction in question shall apply with such modification as may be
necessary to make it valid.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">12.5.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Sellers acknowledge that the above provisions of this clause are no more extensive than
is reasonable to protect the Purchaser as the purchaser of the Shares.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">12.6.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The covenants in this clause may be enforced with the prior written consent of the Purchaser
by each Group Company against the Sellers under the Contracts (Rights of Third Parties) Act
1999. The provisions of this clause may be varied or terminated by Agreement between the
Sellers and the Purchaser (which may also release or compromise any liability in whole or in
part) without the consent of any Group Company.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>13.&nbsp;SHARE REPURCHASE</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">13.1. The parties hereto agree to comply with the provisions of the Share Repurchase Agreement.


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>It is agreed that the provisions of the Share Repurchase Agreement shall also apply to any
other securities for the time being representing or derived from the Consideration Shares
governed by the Share Repurchase Agreement (whether by way of consolidation, subdivision,
capitalisation or rights issue or otherwise), other than any such securities as may be
acquired for cash by way of rights or other issue.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>14.&nbsp;CONFIDENTIALITY</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">14.1.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>No party shall make or permit any person connected with them to make any announcement
concerning this sale and purchase or any ancillary matter before, on or after Completion.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">14.2. Each Seller shall:

Purchaser or otherwise obtained by or in connection with this Agreement which relates
to any member of the Purchaser Group; and</TD>
</TR>

<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>if after Completion a Seller holds confidential information relating to any
Group Company, it shall keep that information confidential and, to the extent
reasonably practicable, shall return that information to the Purchaser or destroy it,
in each case without retaining copies.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">14.3.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Nothing in this clause prevents any announcement being made or any confidential information
being disclosed:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>with the written approval of the other parties, which in the case of any
announcement shall not be unreasonably withheld or delayed; or</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>

the avoidance of doubt, any &#147;recognised investment exchange&#148;, as such expression is
defined in the UK Financial Services and Markets Act 2000 (as amended)), but a party
required to disclose any confidential information shall promptly notify the other
parties, where practicable and lawful to do so, before disclosure occurs and co-operate
with the other parties regarding the timing and content of such disclosure or any
action which the other parties may reasonably elect to take to challenge the validity
of such requirement,</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">14.4. Nothing in this clause prevents disclosure of confidential information by any party:

adheres to those terms as if he were bound by the provisions of this clause.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>17.&nbsp;FURTHER ASSURANCES</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">17.1.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>On or after Completion, each Seller shall, at their own cost and expense, execute and do (or
procure to be executed and done by any other necessary party) all such deeds, documents, acts
and things as the Purchaser may from time to time reasonably require in order to transfer any
of the Shares in the Purchaser or its assignee or as otherwise may be reasonably necessary to
give full effect to this Agreement.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">17.2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In relation to each Group Company, the Sellers shall procure the convening of all meetings,
the giving of all waivers and consents and the passing of all resolutions as are necessary
under the Companies Act 1985, its articles of association or any agreement or obligation
affecting it to give effect to this Agreement.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">17.3.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>For so long after Completion as any Seller or any nominee remains the registered holder of
any Share, they shall hold (and direct any nominee to hold) that Share and any distributions,
property and rights deriving from it on trust for the Purchaser and shall deal with the Shares
and any distributions, property and rights deriving from them as the Purchaser directs; in
particular, each Seller shall exercise all voting rights as the Purchaser directs or shall
execute an instrument of proxy or other document which enables the Purchaser or its
representative to attend and vote at any meeting of the Company.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>18.&nbsp;ASSIGNMENTS</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">18.1.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Purchaser may assign the benefit of this Agreement and the Tax Deed to any member of the
Purchaser Group and if it does so:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the assignee may enforce the obligations on the part of the Sellers (including
the Warranties) under this Agreement and under the Tax Deed as if it had been named in
this Agreement and in the Tax Deed as the Purchaser;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>as between the Sellers and the Purchaser, the Sellers may nevertheless enforce
this Agreement and the Tax Deed against the Purchaser as if that assignment had not
occurred;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the assignment shall not in any way operate so as to increase or reduce the
respective rights and obligations on the part of the Purchaser or its assignee on the
one hand and the Sellers on the other hand; and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>if the assignee ceases to be a member of the Purchaser Group, the Purchaser
shall procure that the benefit of this Agreement and the Tax Deed is re-assigned to the
Purchaser or another member of the Purchaser Group prior to it ceasing to be a member
of the Purchaser Group.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">18.2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Except as permitted by this clause, none of the rights or obligations under this Agreement
or the Tax Deed may be assigned or transferred without the prior consent of both the Sellers
and the Purchaser.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>

the Tax Deed, it shall pay interest on that sum from the date on which payment is due until
the date of actual payment (after as well as before judgment) at an annual rate of four per
cent (4%) above the base rate from time to time of Barclays Bank plc, which interest shall
accrue from day to day and be compounded monthly.</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If any Seller is required by law to make a deduction or withholding in respect of any sum
payable under this Agreement, they shall, at the same time as the sum which is the subject of
the deduction or withholding is payable, pay to the Purchaser such additional amount as shall
be required to ensure that the net amount received by the Purchaser will equal the full amount
which would have been received by it had no such deduction or withholding been required to be
made.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>20.&nbsp;GENERAL</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">20.1.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The receipt by the Sellers&#146; Solicitors of any sum or document to be paid or delivered to a
Seller will discharge the Purchaser&#146;s obligation to pay or deliver it to that Seller.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">20.2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each of the obligations and undertakings set out in this Agreement (excluding any obligation
which is fully performed at Completion) shall continue in force after Completion and will not
be affected by the waiver of any Condition or any notice given by the Purchaser in respect of
any Condition.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">20.3.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Sellers agree to appoint a &#147;<U>Sellers&#146; Agent</U>&#148; immediately following Completion on
such terms as would permit to the fullest extent reasonably possible such person to give any
consents or waivers on behalf of all of the Sellers.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">20.4.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each party shall pay the costs and expenses incurred by it in connection with the entering
into and completion of this Agreement.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">20.5.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This Agreement may be executed in any number of counterparts. This has the same effect as
if the signatures on the counterparts were on a single copy of this Agreement. The parties
may exchange their respective counterparts by telecopier.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">20.6. The rights of each party under this Agreement:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">(a)&nbsp;may be exercised as often as necessary;



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">(b)&nbsp;are cumulative and not exclusive of rights and remedies provided by law; and



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">(c)&nbsp;may be waived only in writing and specifically.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:8%; font-size: 12pt">Delay in exercising or non-exercise of any such right is not a waiver of that right.


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">20.7.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Except as expressly stated in this Agreement, a person who is not a party to this Agreement
may not enforce any of its terms under the Contracts (Rights of Third Parties) Act 1999.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">20.8.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Seller hereby represents, warrants and undertakes that he has no right of claim of
whatsoever nature against the Company or any of its present or former officers, employees or
members. To the extent that any such claim exists or may exist, each Seller hereby
irrevocably waives such claim, releases each such person from any liability whatsoever in
respect of such claim and fully indemnifies and holds harmless each such person and the
Purchaser against any loss, liability or cost incurred in connection with the same.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>21.&nbsp;WHOLE AGREEMENT</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">21.1.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This Agreement, together with the Share Repurchase Agreement, the Tax Deed, the Registration
Rights Agreement, the Disclosure Letter, the Data Room&nbsp;Escrow, the Escrow Agreement, and the
Release Account Escrow Agreement contains the whole agreement between the parties relating to
the transactions contemplated by this agreement and supersedes all previous agreements between
the parties relating to these transactions. The parties hereby irrevocably terminate the term
sheet entered into by them in October&nbsp;2004 and the non-disclosure agreement dated 1 October
2004. For the avoidance of doubt, the Investment Agreement is irrevocably terminated by the
Sellers.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">21.2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each party acknowledges that in agreeing to enter into this Agreement they have not relied
on any representation, warranty, collateral contract or other assurance (except those set out
in this Agreement made by or on behalf of any other party before the signature of this
Agreement. Each party waives all rights and remedies which, but for this subclause, might
otherwise be available to them in respect of any such representation, warranty, collateral
contract or other assurance.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">21.3. Nothing in the preceeding subclause limits or excludes any liability for fraud.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">1.1 <B>Accuracy of recitals and schedules</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">The particulars relating to the Group Companies and the Properties set out in the recitals
and the schedules to this Agreement are true and accurate.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">1.2 <B>Memorandum and articles of association, statutory books and returns</B>

</TR>

</TABLE>

to give or create any of the foregoing, and no person has claimed to be entitled to any
of the foregoing.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">1.7 <B>Compliance with statutes</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">No Group Company, nor any of its officers, agents or employees (during the course of their
duties), has done or omitted to do anything which is a contravention of any statute, order,
regulation or the like giving rise to any fine, penalty or other liability or sanction on
the part of that Group Company.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">1.8 <B>Licences and consents</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">To the best of Sellers&#146; knowledge, Each Group Company has all licences (including statutory
licences) and consents necessary to own and operate its assets and to carry on its business
as it does at present and none of the Sellers is aware of anything that might result in the
revocation, suspension or modification of any of those licences or consents or that might
prejudice their renewal.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">2.&nbsp;<B>ACCOUNTS AND FINANCIAL</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">2.1 <B>Accuracy of Accounts</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">The Accounts:

date change have had any impact upon the performance or functionality of the Systems up to
and including the date of this Agreement and neither the year 2000 date change nor any
subsequent date change will have any impact on the performance or functionality of the
Systems after that date.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">&#147;<U>Euro Compliant</U>&#148; means that during and after the introduction of any new currency in
connection with European Economic and Monetary Union:

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">4.&nbsp;<B>TAXATION</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">&#147;<U>Taxation</U>&#148; or &#147;<U>Tax</U>&#148; means any form of taxation, duty, impost, levy, tariff in the
nature of taxation imposed by any country (or any territory, state, municipality or any other
political sub-division thereof) whether or not any such taxation, duty, impost, levy or tariff
arises in respect of actual or deemed, gross or net income, profit, gain, value, receipt, payment,
sale, use, issue of capital, transfer, acquisition or production of assets, occupation, franchise,
value added, property or right and any penalty, charge, surcharge, fine or interest payable in
connection with any such taxation, duty, impost, levy or tariff;


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">&#147;<U>Tax Authority</U>&#148; means any authority or body, in any jurisdiction and whether national or
otherwise having the power or authority to collect or impose Tax;


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">&#147;<U>Tax Statute</U>&#148; means any primary or secondary statute, instrument, enactment, order, law,
by-law or regulation in any jurisdiction imposing Tax;

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">6.&nbsp;<B>EMPLOYEES</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">6.1 <B>Interpretation</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">In this section of this schedule headed &#147;Employees&#148;:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">&#147;<U>Relevant Period</U>&#148; means, unless otherwise expressly provided, the three years before
the date of this Agreement.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">&#147;<U>Representative Body</U>&#148; means any association, trade union, works council or any other
body or persons representing any of the Group Companies&#146; workers.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">&#147;<U>Retirement/Death/Disability Benefit</U>&#148; means any pension, lump sum, gratuity or other
like benefit given or to be given on retirement or on death, or in anticipation of
retirement, or, in connection with past service, after retirement or death, or to be given
on or in anticipation of or in connection with any change in the nature of the service of
the worker in question or given or to be given on or in connection with the illness, injury
or disability of, or suffering of any accident by, a worker.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">&#147;<U>worker</U>&#148; means all employees, including directors and officers of any Group Company.

<P align="center" style="font-size: 12pt"><U><B>SCHEDULE 6</B></U>



<P align="center" style="font-size: 12pt"><U><B>LIMITS ON WARRANTY CLAIMS</B></U>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>1.&nbsp;Exclusions</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">The Sellers shall not be liable in respect of a Warranty Claim:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>for which provision is made, or of which the payment or discharge is reflected,
in the Accounts; or</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>which would not have arisen but for a change in legislation announced after
Completion (whether relating to taxation, rates of taxation or otherwise) or the
withdrawal of any extra statutory concession previously made by the Inland Revenue or
other taxing authority (whether or not the change purports to be effective
retrospectively in whole or in part); or</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>which would not have arisen but for a change after Completion in the accounting
bases upon which any Group Company values its assets (other than a change made in order
to comply with UK GAAP);</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>for which the Purchaser is compensated as a result of a claim under the Tax
Deed;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">(e)&nbsp;for which payment is received under an insurance policy; or


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(f)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>which has been fairly disclosed in the Disclosure Letter or in the Data Room
Information; or</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(g)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>which is for any indirect or consequential loss or damage or punitive damage
including any loss of profits, business or anticipated savings, whether arising from
negligence, breach of contract or otherwise on the part of the Purchaser; or</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(h)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>which relates to facts or circumstances that occurred after Completion (but
which did not originate or have a cause that occurred before Completion) other than
through the negligence, misrepresentation, fraud, or dishonesty of the Sellers (or any
of them or their agents or advisors) or a breach by the Sellers (or any of them) of
clause 10.1 of the Agreement).</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>2.&nbsp;Threshold</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">The Sellers shall not be liable in respect of any Warranty Claim unless the amount of all
Warranty Claims, when aggregated with any and/or all claims made under the Tax Deed (or all
such claims which might have been made but for the previous operation of this paragraph or
the corresponding provision in the Tax Deed), exceeds $10,000, in which case the whole
amount may be recovered by the Purchaser.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>3.&nbsp;Aggregate limit</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">Except as provided in this schedule, the maximum aggregate liability of the Sellers in
respect of the Warranties and under the Tax Deed shall not exceed seventy percent (70%) of
the Warranty Liability Amount.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">That limit on the maximum aggregate liability of the Sellers shall be increased by:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(i)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any amount received by any Seller under the paragraph below headed &#147;Recovery
from third parties&#148;; and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(j)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the amount of any interest payable by any Seller in respect of any late payment
under this Agreement or the Tax Deed.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>4.&nbsp;Time limits</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">The liability of the Sellers in respect of the Warranties shall terminate (but without
prejudice to the rights and obligations of the parties under the Tax Deed):


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>on the seventh anniversary of Completion in respect of those matters set out in
Part&nbsp;D (Taxation) of Schedule&nbsp;5 and any other matters so far as they relate to
taxation; and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>two (2)&nbsp;years after Completion in respect of all other matters contained in
Schedule&nbsp;5.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">except in respect of any Warranty Claim of which notice is given to the Sellers or the
Sellers&#146; Solicitors before the relevant date. The liability of the Sellers in respect of
any Warranty Claim shall in any event terminate if proceedings in respect of it have not
been commenced within twelve (12)&nbsp;months of service of notice of that Warranty Claim unless
the Sellers shall have assumed conduct of the claim in question in accordance with the
provisions of this schedule or the Tax Deed.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>5.&nbsp;Notice of Warranty Claims</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>At the date hereof, other than as set forth in the Disclosure Letter the
Purchaser declares not to be aware of any matter which could lead to liability of the
Seller in respect of a Warranty Claim.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If the Purchaser or any of the Group Companies becomes aware of a matter which
is likely to give rise to a Warranty Claim, the Purchaser shall give notice of the
relevant facts to the Sellers as soon as reasonably practicable after becoming aware of
those facts.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">(c)&nbsp;The foregoing shall not affect any indemnification obligation of the Sellers.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>6.&nbsp;Conduct of third party claims</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">If a Warranty Claim arises as a result of, or in connection with, a liability or alleged
liability to a third party (a &#147;<U>Third Party Claim</U>&#148;), then (subject to the provisions
of the Tax Deed in relation to any matter which is the subject of a claim under it) the
Sellers may elect to assume the conduct of any appeal, dispute, compromise or defence of the
Third Party Claim and of any incidental negotiations on the following terms:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Sellers shall first indemnify and secure the Purchaser and the relevant
Group Company to the Purchasers reasonable satisfaction against all liabilities,
charges, costs and expenses which they may incur in taking any such action as the
Sellers may require;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Purchaser shall procure the relevant Group Company to make available to the
Sellers such persons and all such information as the Sellers may reasonably require for
assessing, contesting, appealing or compromising the Third Party Claim;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Purchaser shall procure that the relevant Group Company takes such action
to contest, appeal or compromise the Third Party Claim as may be requested by the
Sellers and does not make any admission of liability, agreement, settlement or
compromise in relation to the Third Party Claim without the approval of the Sellers;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Sellers shall keep the Purchaser promptly informed of the progress of the
Third Party Claim and provide the Purchaser with copies of all relevant documents and
such other information in their possession as may be requested by the Purchaser; and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(e)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>but nothing in this paragraph shall require the Purchaser to do anything which
in the reasonable opinion of the Purchaser would be prejudicial in any material respect
to the goodwill of the business of any Group Company or any member of the Purchaser
Group or to their commercial interests as the owner of any such business.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>7.&nbsp;Mitigation</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">Nothing in this Agreement shall be deemed to relieve the Purchaser from any duty whether in
common law or otherwise to mitigate any loss or damage incurred by it as a result of any
breach of the Warranties.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>8.&nbsp;Recovery from third parties</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">This paragraph applies if:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any Seller makes a payment (excluding any interest on a late payment) in
respect of a Warranty Claim (the &#147;<U>Damages Payment</U>&#148;); and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>within twelve (12)&nbsp;months of the making of the relevant payment any Group
Company or the Purchaser receives any sum other than from another Seller which would
not have been received but for the circumstance which gave rise to that Warranty Claim
(the &#147;<U>Third Party Sum</U>&#148;); and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the receipt of the Third Party Sum was not taken into account in calculating
the Damages Payment; and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the aggregate of the Third Party Sum and the Damages Payment exceeds the amount
required to compensate the Purchaser in full for the loss or liability which gave rise
to the Warranty Claim in question, such excess being the &#147;<U>Excess Recovery</U>&#148;.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">If this paragraph applies, the Purchaser shall, promptly on receipt of the Third Party Sum
by it or the relevant Group Company, repay to that Seller an amount equal to the lower of
(i)&nbsp;the Excess Recovery and (ii)&nbsp;the Damages Payment, after deducting (in either case) all
costs incurred by the Purchaser or the relevant Group Company in recovering the Third Party
Sum and any taxation payable by the Purchaser or any Group Company by virtue of its receipt.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>9.&nbsp;Scope of limitations</B>



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">Nothing in this schedule or in the Disclosure Letter shall qualify or limit the liability of
the Sellers in relation to:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:4%; font-size: 12pt">(a)&nbsp;those Warranties set out in paragraphs 1.3 and 1.12 of Schedule&nbsp;5; or


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any Warranty Claim attributable to the fraud, dishonesty or wilful concealment
on the part of the Sellers or their agents or advisers.</TD>
</TR>


</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; display: none">11
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->


<P><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 12pt">



</TABLE>

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">This schedule has been omitted pursuant to Item&nbsp;601(b)(2) of Regulation&nbsp;S-K. This schedule
consists of a description of the conduct of the parties prior to the closing of the transaction.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; display: none">12
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->


<P align="center" style="font-size: 12pt"><U><B>SCHEDULE 8</B></U>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">This schedule has been omitted pursuant to Item&nbsp;601(b)(2) of Regulation&nbsp;S-K. This schedule
consists of a description of the closing procedures


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; display: none">13
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->


<P align="center" style="font-size: 12pt"><U><B>SCHEDULE 9</B></U>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">This schedule has been omitted pursuant to Item&nbsp;601(b)(2) of Regulation&nbsp;S-K. This schedule would

calculation was necessary at closing; however, no such calculation was necessary in connection with
the closing.

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>WHEREAS</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>&nbsp;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%"><B>&nbsp;</B></TD>
    <TD><B>(</B>A) Chordiant has requested KiQ to cancel certain options held by various option holders
(&#147;<B>Options</B>&#148;);</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">(B)&nbsp;Chordiant is planning to acquire the entire issued share capital of KiQ;


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt">(C)&nbsp;Chordiant wishes to KiQ to hold certain sums on trust for its benefit.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 12pt"><B>NOW THIS DEED WITNESSES AS FOLLOWS:</B>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">1.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Chordiant shall pay the sum of GBP539,475 to KiQ on or immediately before the completion of
the acquisition of the entire issued share capital of KiQ by Chordiant.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>KiQ declares and acknowledges that it shall hold such monies on trust for the exclusive
benefit of Chordiant and shall act exclusively on Chordiant&#146;s directions in respect of the
same. Such monies will be used exclusively for the purposes of cancelling and terminating the
Options.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">3.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This Deed may be executed in any number of counterparts, and by the parties on separate
counterparts, but in that case shall not be effective until each party has agreed to do at
least one counterpart. Each counterpart shall constitute the original of this Deed, but all
the counterparts together with constitute one and the same instrument. The parties agree that
they may exchange their counterparts of this Deed by telecopier.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">4.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This Deed shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of England and
Wales.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">5.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In the event that Chordiant does not complete the acquisition of the entire issued share
capital of KiQ, and that the sum referred to in clause 1 above has been transferred to KiQ on
trust for Chordiant, this sum shall immediately be transferred to Chordiant in accordance with
Chordiant&#146;s instructions.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
